-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="28e5101403c946d4a1c86b11af68853a"><span data-offset-key="28e5101403c946d4a1c86b11af68853a:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://github.com/benoitc/gunicorn" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="8faf7bff36cc4b6e89c7eb3015010f58"><span data-offset-key="8faf7bff36cc4b6e89c7eb3015010f58:0">gunicorn</span></span></a><span data-key="c3a2103d136d47768733c1658301fb17"><span data-offset-key="c3a2103d136d47768733c1658301fb17:0"> - Pre-forked, partly written in C.</span></span></span>

-   <span class="text-4505230f--TextH400-3033861f--textContentFamily-49a318e1"><span data-key="2ee43a5add8d40a8aa0e679742d9d06e"><span data-offset-key="2ee43a5add8d40a8aa0e679742d9d06e:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://uwsgi-docs.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" class="link-a079aa82--primary-53a25e66--link-faf6c434"><span data-key="abd591ad6e2747d1ac9d0303cf62722d"><span data-offset-key="abd591ad6e2747d1ac9d0303cf62722d:0">uWSGI</span></span></a><span data-key="67aa8c7635e64d4f970d917f1985d28a"><span data-offset-key="67aa8c7635e64d4f970d917f1985d28a:0"> - A project aims at developing a full stack for building hosting services, written in C.</span></span></span>
